};

var TOPIC_SHORT_TITLES = {
  "MCI":"NCP-MCI",
  "AI":"NCP-AI",
  "EUC":"NCP-EUC",
  "CN":"NCP-CN",
  "US":"NCP-US",
  "MCA":"NCP-MCA",
  "DB":"NCP-DB",
  "CI":"NCP-CI [AWS]",
};

var TOPIC_ORDER = ["MCI", "AI", "CN", "EUC","US","MCA","DB","CI"];
var currentTopic = "MCI";
var topicStates = {};

var QUESTIONS = QUESTION_BANKS[currentTopic].slice();
var ORIGINAL_QUESTIONS = QUESTIONS.slice();
var index = 0;
var score = 0;
var answeredMap = {};
var selectedMap = {};
var resultMap = {};
var flagMap = {};
var continueUnansweredMode = false;
var reviewCorrectAnswerMode = false;
var correctAnswerReviewResumeIndex = 0;
var reviewAnsweredSnapshot = null;
var reviewSelectedSnapshot = null;
var reviewResultSnapshot = null;
var shuffleMode = false;
var sectionMode = { type:'full', start:1, end:null, label:'Full' };
var sectionPickerSize = 20;
var lastSectionListCount = null;
var jumpOpen = false;
var jumpPanelBodyHeight = null;
var jumpResizePointerId = null;
var jumpResizeStartY = 0;
var jumpResizeStartHeight = 0;
var jumpResizeShouldClose = false;

function isStudyMode(){
  return currentUiMode === 'study';
}

function saveCurrentTopicState() {
  if (isStudyMode()) return;

  topicStates[currentTopic] = {
    QUESTIONS: QUESTIONS.slice(),
    ORIGINAL_QUESTIONS: ORIGINAL_QUESTIONS.slice(),
    index: index,
    score: score,
    answeredMap: answeredMap,
    selectedMap: selectedMap,
    resultMap: resultMap,
    flagMap: flagMap,
    shuffleMode: shuffleMode,
    sectionMode: Object.assign({}, sectionMode)
  };
}

function loadTopicState(topic) {
  currentTopic = topic;
  var saved = topicStates[topic];
  if (saved) {
    QUESTIONS = saved.QUESTIONS.slice();
    ORIGINAL_QUESTIONS = saved.ORIGINAL_QUESTIONS.slice();
    index = saved.index;
    score = saved.score;
    answeredMap = saved.answeredMap;
    selectedMap = saved.selectedMap;
    resultMap = saved.resultMap;
    flagMap = saved.flagMap;
    shuffleMode = saved.shuffleMode;
    sectionMode = saved.sectionMode ? Object.assign({}, saved.sectionMode) : { type:'full', start:1, end:null, label:'Full' };
  } else {
    QUESTIONS = QUESTION_BANKS[topic].slice();
    ORIGINAL_QUESTIONS = QUESTIONS.slice();
    index = 0;
    score = 0;
    answeredMap = {};
    selectedMap = {};
    resultMap = {};
    flagMap = {};
    shuffleMode = false;
    sectionMode = { type:'full', start:1, end:null, label:'Full' };
  }
}

function setUiMode(mode){
  currentUiMode = mode || 'exam';
  updateTopicUI();
}

function updateHeaderBadgeMode(){
  var badge = byId('headerBadge');
  if(!badge) return;

  var mode = currentUiMode || 'exam';

  if(mode === 'summary'){
    badge.textContent = 'SUMMARY';
    badge.style.color = 'var(--green)';
    badge.style.background = 'var(--green-bg)';
    badge.style.borderColor = 'var(--green-bd)';
  }else if(mode === 'flagged'){
    badge.textContent = 'FLAGGED';
    badge.style.color = 'var(--amber)';
    badge.style.background = 'var(--amber-bg)';
    badge.style.borderColor = 'rgba(245,158,11,.35)';
  }else if(mode === 'retake'){
    badge.textContent = 'RETAKE';
    badge.style.color = 'var(--amber)';
    badge.style.background = 'var(--amber-bg)';
    badge.style.borderColor = 'rgba(245,158,11,.35)';
  }else if(mode === 'study'){
    badge.textContent = 'STUDY MODE';
    badge.style.color = 'var(--green)';
    badge.style.background = 'var(--green-bg)';
    badge.style.borderColor = 'var(--green-bd)';
  }else{
    badge.textContent = 'EXAM DUMP';
    badge.style.color = 'var(--blue)';
    badge.style.background = 'var(--blue-bg)';
    badge.style.borderColor = 'var(--blue-bd)';
  }
}

function updateTopicUI() {
  var fullTitle = TOPIC_TITLES[currentTopic] || currentTopic;
  var shortTitle = TOPIC_SHORT_TITLES && TOPIC_SHORT_TITLES[currentTopic]
    ? TOPIC_SHORT_TITLES[currentTopic]
    : ('NCP-' + currentTopic);

  var count = (QUESTIONS || []).length;
  var mode = currentUiMode || 'exam';
  var isRetakeMode = mode === 'retake';
  var isFlaggedMode = mode === 'flagged';
  var isStudy = mode === 'study';

  var ht = byId('headerTitle');
  if (ht) ht.textContent = fullTitle;

  updateHeaderBadgeMode();

  var pickerTitle = byId('examPickerTitle');
  if (pickerTitle) pickerTitle.textContent = shortTitle;

  var pickerSub = byId('examPickerSub');
  if (pickerSub) {
    if(isFlaggedMode){
      pickerSub.textContent = count + ' Flagged Questions';
    }else if(isRetakeMode){
      pickerSub.textContent = count + ' Retake Questions';
    }else if(isStudy){
      pickerSub.textContent = 'Study Mode - ' + count + ' Questions';
    }else{
      var sectionText = sectionMode && sectionMode.type === 'range' ? sectionMode.label + ' • ' : '';
      pickerSub.textContent = sectionText + count + ' Questions';
    }
  }

  var sectionVal = byId('statSection');
  if(sectionVal){
    if(isRetakeMode){
      sectionVal.textContent = 'Retake';
    }else if(sectionMode && sectionMode.type === 'range'){
      sectionVal.textContent = 'Q' + sectionMode.start + '-' + sectionMode.end;
    }else{
      sectionVal.textContent = 'Full';
    }
  }

  document.querySelectorAll('.exam-menu-item').forEach(function(btn) {
    if (btn.getAttribute('data-topic') === currentTopic) btn.classList.add('active');
    else btn.classList.remove('active');
  });

  var shuffleBtn = byId('shuffleBtn');
  if (shuffleBtn) {
    if (shuffleMode) shuffleBtn.classList.add('on');
    else shuffleBtn.classList.remove('on');
  }
}

function shortTopicTitle(topic) {
  return 'NCP-' + topic;
}

function cleanTopicName(topic) {
  var title = TOPIC_TITLES[topic] || topic;
  return title.replace(/^NCP-/, '').replace(/\s*6\.10$/, '');
}

function examIcon(topic) {
  var icons = {};
  return icons[topic] || topic.slice(0,2);
}

function renderLandingSummary() {
  var totalExams = TOPIC_ORDER.length;
  var mini = byId('landingMiniStat');
  if (mini) mini.textContent = totalExams + ' Exams';
}

function renderHomeExamCards() {
  var grid = byId('homeExamGrid');
  if (!grid) return;
  grid.innerHTML = '';
  renderLandingSummary();

  TOPIC_ORDER.forEach(function(topic) {
    var count = (QUESTION_BANKS[topic] || []).length;
    var card = document.createElement('div');
    card.className = 'exam-card';
    card.setAttribute('role', 'button');
    card.setAttribute('tabindex', '0');
    card.setAttribute('aria-label', shortTopicTitle(topic) + ', choose study or practice mode');
    card.innerHTML =
      '<span class="exam-card-icon">' + escHtml(examIcon(topic)) + '</span>' +
      '<span class="exam-card-main">' +
        '<span class="exam-card-code">' + escHtml(shortTopicTitle(topic)) + '</span>' +
        '<span class="exam-card-name">' + escHtml(cleanTopicName(topic)) + '</span>' +
      '</span>' +
      '<span class="exam-card-side">' +
        '<span class="exam-card-count">' + count + ' Qns</span>' +
        '<span class="exam-card-arrow">›</span>' +
      '</span>';
    card.onclick = function(){ openLandingModeModal(topic); };
    card.onkeydown = function(evt){
      if(evt.key === 'Enter' || evt.key === ' '){
        evt.preventDefault();
        openLandingModeModal(topic);
      }
    };
    grid.appendChild(card);
  });
}

var pendingLandingTopic = null;

function openLandingModeModal(topic){
  if(!QUESTION_BANKS[topic]) return;
  pendingLandingTopic = topic;

  var count = (QUESTION_BANKS[topic] || []).length;
  var icon = byId('landingModeIcon');
  var code = byId('landingModeCode');
  var name = byId('landingModeName');
  var total = byId('landingModeCount');
  var modal = byId('landingModeModal');

  if(icon) icon.textContent = examIcon(topic);
  if(code) code.textContent = shortTopicTitle(topic);
  if(name) name.textContent = cleanTopicName(topic);
  if(total) total.textContent = count + ' Qns';
  if(modal) modal.classList.remove('hidden');
}

function closeLandingModeModal(){
  var modal = byId('landingModeModal');
  if(modal) modal.classList.add('hidden');
}

function startLandingMode(intent){
  if(!pendingLandingTopic) return;
  var topic = pendingLandingTopic;
  pendingLandingTopic = null;
  closeLandingModeModal();
  startExam(topic, intent);
}

function prepareStudySession() {
  reviewCorrectAnswerMode = false;
  continueUnansweredMode = false;
  selectedMap = {};
  answeredMap = {};
  resultMap = {};
  score = 0;
  index = 0;
  if(typeof setUiMode === 'function') setUiMode('study');
}

function enterExamDumpFromStudy(){
  reviewCorrectAnswerMode = false;
  continueUnansweredMode = false;
  selectedMap = {};
  answeredMap = {};
  resultMap = {};
  score = 0;
  index = 0;

  if(typeof setUiMode === 'function') setUiMode('exam');

  var result = byId('resultCard');
  if(result){
    result.classList.remove('show');
    result.innerHTML = '';
  }

  var qCard = byId('questionCard');
  var controls = byId('controlsWrap');
  if(qCard) qCard.classList.remove('hidden');
  if(controls) controls.classList.remove('hidden');

  renderQuestion();
  scrollToTop();
}

function openStudyExitConfirm(){
  var modal = byId('studyExitConfirmModal');
  if(modal) modal.classList.remove('hidden');
}

function closeStudyExitConfirm(){
  var modal = byId('studyExitConfirmModal');
  if(modal) modal.classList.add('hidden');
}

function confirmEnterExamDumpFromStudy(){
  closeStudyExitConfirm();
  enterExamDumpFromStudy();
}

function updateStudyToggleMenuItem(){
  var btn = byId('moreStudyToggleBtn');
  var icon = byId('moreStudyToggleIcon');
  var label = byId('moreStudyToggleLabel');
  if(!btn || !label) return;

  var canToggle = currentUiMode === 'exam' || currentUiMode === 'study';
  btn.classList.toggle('hidden', !canToggle);

  if(isStudyMode()){
    if(icon) icon.textContent = '↩';
    label.textContent = 'Exam Dump Mode';
  }else{
    if(icon) icon.textContent = '✓';
    label.textContent = 'Study Mode';
  }
}

function toggleStudyModeFromMore(){
  if(currentUiMode !== 'exam' && currentUiMode !== 'study') return;

  reviewCorrectAnswerMode = false;
  continueUnansweredMode = false;

  if(isStudyMode()){
    if(typeof setUiMode === 'function') setUiMode('exam');
  }else{
    if(typeof setUiMode === 'function') setUiMode('study');
  }

  var result = byId('resultCard');
  if(result){
    result.classList.remove('show');
    result.innerHTML = '';
  }

  var qCard = byId('questionCard');
  var controls = byId('controlsWrap');
  if(qCard) qCard.classList.remove('hidden');
  if(controls) controls.classList.remove('hidden');

  var menu = byId('moreMenu');
  if(menu) menu.classList.add('hidden');

  renderQuestion();
  scrollToTop();
}

function startExam(topic, intent) {
  if (!QUESTION_BANKS[topic]) return;

  var studyIntent = intent === 'study';

  saveCurrentTopicState();
  loadTopicState(topic);

  if (studyIntent) {
    prepareStudySession();
  } else if(typeof setUiMode === 'function') {
    setUiMode('exam');
  }

  document.body.classList.remove('home-mode');
  closeExamMenu();
  closeDropdown();
  var search = byId('searchInput');
  if (search) search.value = '';
  updateTopicUI();
  renderQuestion();
  scrollToTop();
}

function toggleExamMenu() {
  var menu = byId('examMenu');
  var picker = byId('examPicker');
  var btn = byId('examPickerBtn');
  if (!menu) return;
  var isHidden = menu.classList.contains('hidden');
  if (isHidden) {
    menu.classList.remove('hidden');
    if (picker) picker.classList.add('open');
    if (btn) btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
  } else {
    menu.classList.add('hidden');
    if (picker) picker.classList.remove('open');
    if (btn) btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
  }
}

function closeExamMenu() {
  var menu = byId('examMenu');
  var picker = byId('examPicker');
  var btn = byId('examPickerBtn');
  if (menu) menu.classList.add('hidden');
  if (picker) picker.classList.remove('open');
  if (btn) btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
}

function selectTopicFromMenu(topic) {
  var keepStudy = isStudyMode();
  closeExamMenu();
  switchTopic(topic, keepStudy ? 'study' : 'practice');
}

function switchTopic(topic, intent) {
  if (!QUESTION_BANKS[topic]) return;
  if (topic === currentTopic) return;

  var studyIntent = intent === 'study';

  saveCurrentTopicState();
  loadTopicState(topic);

  if (studyIntent) {
    prepareStudySession();
  } else if(typeof setUiMode === 'function') {
    setUiMode('exam');
  }

  closeDropdown();
  closeExamMenu();
  byId('searchInput').value = '';
  updateTopicUI();
  renderQuestion();
  scrollToTop();
}

function renderExamMenu() {
  var menu = byId('examMenu');
  if (!menu) return;

  menu.innerHTML = '';

  TOPIC_ORDER.forEach(function(topic) {
    var count = (QUESTION_BANKS[topic] || []).length;
    var btn = document.createElement('button');

    btn.className = 'exam-menu-item';
    btn.type = 'button';
    btn.setAttribute('data-topic', topic);

    btn.onclick = function() {
      selectTopicFromMenu(topic);
    };

    btn.innerHTML =
      '<span class="exam-menu-name">' + escHtml(shortTopicTitle(topic)) + '</span>' +
      '<span class="exam-menu-count">' + count + ' Questions</span>';

    menu.appendChild(btn);
  });
}

window.addEventListener('load', function(){
  setJumpPanelOpen(false);
  initJumpPanelResize();

  renderExamMenu();
  updateTopicUI();
  renderHomeExamCards();
});

document.addEventListener('click', function(e){
  var picker = byId('examPicker');
  if (picker && !picker.contains(e.target)) closeExamMenu();
});

function byId(id) { return document.getElementById(id); }
function questionKeyAt(idx){
  return getQuestionKeyAt(idx);
}
function currentKey() { return questionKeyAt(index); }
function escHtml(value) {
  return String(value).replace(/[&<>"']/g, function(c) {
    return ({'&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;'})[c];
  });
}
function correctAnswers(q) { return String(q.answer || '').toLowerCase().match(/[a-d]/g) || []; }
function requiredCount(q) { var a = correctAnswers(q); return a.length > 0 ? a.length : 1; }
function currentSelections() {
  var key = currentKey();
  if (!selectedMap[key]) selectedMap[key] = [];
  return selectedMap[key];
}
function setSelections(arr) { selectedMap[currentKey()] = arr; }

function renderQuestion() {
  var q = QUESTIONS[index];
  var req = requiredCount(q);
  var selected = currentSelections();
  var rawDone = !!answeredMap[currentKey()];
  var reviewReveal = !!reviewCorrectAnswerMode;
  var studyReveal = isStudyMode();
  var done = rawDone || reviewReveal || studyReveal;
  var isReviewUnanswered = reviewReveal && !rawDone;
  var pct = Math.round(((index + 1) / QUESTIONS.length) * 100);
  var questionCard = byId('questionCard');
  questionCard.classList.remove('hidden');
  questionCard.classList.toggle('flagged', !!flagMap[currentKey()]);
  byId('resultCard').classList.remove('show');
  byId('controlsWrap').classList.remove('hidden');
  byId('metaQnum').textContent = 'Q' + (index + 1);
  var multi = byId('metaMulti');
  if (req > 1) { multi.textContent = 'Choose ' + req; multi.classList.remove('hidden'); }
  else multi.classList.add('hidden');
  byId('questionText').innerHTML = formatQuestionWithDiagram(q);
  byId('progressBar').style.width = pct + '%';
  var box = byId('optionsBox');
  box.innerHTML = '';
  Object.keys(q.options).forEach(function(displayLetter) {
    var originalLetter = ((q._optionMap && q._optionMap[displayLetter]) ? q._optionMap[displayLetter] : displayLetter).toLowerCase();
    var isSelected = selected.indexOf(originalLetter) !== -1;
    var isCorrect = correctAnswers(q).indexOf(originalLetter) !== -1;
    var cls = 'option';
    if (!done && isSelected) cls += ' selected';
    if (done && isCorrect) cls += ' correct';
    if (done && rawDone && isSelected && !isCorrect && !studyReveal) cls += ' wrong';
    var btn = document.createElement('button');
    btn.type = 'button';
    btn.className = cls;
    btn.setAttribute('data-answer', originalLetter);
    if (done) btn.disabled = true;
	btn.innerHTML =
	  '<span class="opt-letter">' + displayLetter + '</span>' +
	  '<span class="opt-text">' + formatRichText(q.options[displayLetter]) + '</span>';
    if (!done) btn.onclick = function() { chooseAnswer(this.getAttribute('data-answer')); };
    box.appendChild(btn);
  });
  var note = byId('answerNote');
  if (!done) {
    if (req === 1) {
      note.textContent = selected.length === 1
        ? 'Ready to submit.'
        : 'Select an answer, then submit.';
    } else {
      note.textContent = selected.length + ' / ' + req + ' selected. Select exactly ' + req + ' answers to submit.';
    }
  } else if (studyReveal) {
    note.textContent = 'Study Mode - correct answer is shown.';
  } else if (isReviewUnanswered) {
    note.textContent = 'Unanswered — correct answer is displayed.';
  } else if (reviewReveal) {
    note.textContent = resultMap[currentKey()] ? 'Correct — answer is displayed.' : 'Wrong — correct answer is displayed.';
  } else {
    note.textContent = '';
  }
  byId('backBtn').disabled = index === 0;
  var skip = byId('skipBtn');
  if (studyReveal) {
    skip.classList.add('hidden');
  } else if (reviewCorrectAnswerMode) {
    skip.classList.remove('hidden');
    skip.disabled = index >= QUESTIONS.length - 1;
    skip.textContent = 'Next →';
  } else if (continueUnansweredMode) {
    skip.classList.remove('hidden');
    skip.disabled = false;
    skip.textContent = nextUnansweredTargetFrom(index) !== -1 ? 'Unanswered' : 'Summary';
  } else {
    skip.classList.remove('hidden');
    skip.disabled = done;
    skip.textContent = 'Skip';
  }

  var submit = byId('submitBtn');
  if (studyReveal) {
    submit.disabled = false;
    submit.textContent = index >= QUESTIONS.length - 1 ? 'Exam Dump' : 'Next \u2192';
  } else if (done) {
    submit.disabled = false;
    if (reviewCorrectAnswerMode) {
      submit.textContent = 'Summary';
    } else if (continueUnansweredMode) {
      submit.textContent = index === QUESTIONS.length - 1 ? 'Finish' : 'Next →';
    } else {
      submit.textContent = index === QUESTIONS.length - 1 ? 'Finish' : 'Next →';
    }
  }
  else { submit.disabled = selected.length !== req; submit.textContent = 'Submit'; }
  var flag = byId('flagBtn');
  if (flagMap[currentKey()]) flag.classList.add('flagged'); else flag.classList.remove('flagged');
  updateTopicUI();
  updateStudyToggleMenuItem();
  updateStats();
  renderJumpButtons();

  setFlagCountForCurrentPool();
}

function animateSubmittedOptions(){
  var options = document.querySelectorAll('.option');

  options.forEach(function(option){
    option.classList.remove('reveal-correct', 'reveal-wrong', 'reveal-selected');

    void option.offsetWidth;

    if(option.classList.contains('correct')){
      option.classList.add('reveal-correct');
    } else if(option.classList.contains('wrong')){
      option.classList.add('reveal-wrong');
    } else if(option.classList.contains('selected')){
      option.classList.add('reveal-selected');
    }
  });
}

function clearQuestionCardAnimations(){
  var card = document.getElementById('questionCard');
  if(!card) return null;

  card.classList.remove(
    'shuffle-refresh',
    'search-jump',
    'slide-out-left',
    'slide-out-right',
    'slide-in-left',
    'slide-in-right',
    'slide-active'
  );

  return card;
}

function animateShuffleRefresh(){
  var card = clearQuestionCardAnimations();
  if(!card) return;

  void card.offsetWidth;
  card.classList.add('shuffle-refresh');
}

function animateSearchJump(){
  var card = clearQuestionCardAnimations();
  if(!card) return;

  void card.offsetWidth;
  card.classList.add('search-jump');
}


var isQuestionAnimating = false;

function animateQuestionChange(direction, changeFn){
  if(isQuestionAnimating) return;

  var card = document.getElementById('questionCard');
  if(!card){
    changeFn();
    return;
  }

  isQuestionAnimating = true;

  var outClass = direction === 'next' ? 'slide-out-left' : 'slide-out-right';
  var inClass = direction === 'next' ? 'slide-in-right' : 'slide-in-left';

  card.classList.remove(
    'slide-out-left',
    'slide-out-right',
    'slide-in-left',
    'slide-in-right',
    'slide-active'
  );

  card.classList.add(outClass);

  setTimeout(function(){
    changeFn();

    card.classList.remove(outClass);
    card.classList.add(inClass);

    requestAnimationFrame(function(){
      card.classList.add('slide-active');
      card.classList.remove(inClass);
    });

    setTimeout(function(){
      card.classList.remove('slide-active');
      isQuestionAnimating = false;
    }, 240);
  }, 160);
}

function chooseAnswer(value) {
  if (isStudyMode()) return;
  if (answeredMap[currentKey()]) return;
  var req = requiredCount(QUESTIONS[index]);
  var selected = currentSelections().slice();
  if (req === 1) selected = [value];
  else {
    var pos = selected.indexOf(value);
    if (pos !== -1) selected.splice(pos, 1);
    else {
      if (selected.length >= req) { byId('answerNote').textContent = 'This question requires exactly ' + req + ' answers.'; return; }
      selected.push(value);
    }
  }
  setSelections(selected);
  renderQuestion();
}

function submitAnswer() {
  if (isStudyMode()) return;
  if (answeredMap[currentKey()]) return;
  var q = QUESTIONS[index];
  var req = requiredCount(q);
  var selected = currentSelections();
  if (selected.length !== req) {
    byId('answerNote').textContent = req === 1 ? 'You must select 1 answer before submitting.' : 'You must select exactly ' + req + ' answers. Selected: ' + selected.length + '/' + req + '.';
    return;
  }
  var correct = correctAnswers(q).sort().join('');
  var chosen = selected.slice().sort().join('');
  var isCorrect = correct === chosen;
  var key = currentKey();
  answeredMap[key] = true;
  resultMap[key] = isCorrect;
  if (isCorrect) score++;
  renderQuestion();

  requestAnimationFrame(function(){
    animateSubmittedOptions();
  });
}
function firstUnansweredIndex() {
  for (var i = 0; i < QUESTIONS.length; i++) {
    if (!answeredMap[getQuestionKeyAt(i)]) return i;
  }
  return -1;
}

function nextUnansweredIndexAfter(startIdx) {
  for (var i = startIdx + 1; i < QUESTIONS.length; i++) {
    if (!answeredMap[getQuestionKeyAt(i)]) return i;
  }
  return -1;
}

function hasNextUnansweredAfter(startIdx) {
  return nextUnansweredIndexAfter(startIdx) !== -1;
}

function nextUnansweredTargetFrom(startIdx) {
  var next = nextUnansweredIndexAfter(startIdx);
  if (next !== -1) return next;

  for (var i = 0; i < startIdx; i++) {
    if (!answeredMap[getQuestionKeyAt(i)]) return i;
  }

  return -1;
}

function nextQuestion() {
  if (isStudyMode()) {
    if (index < QUESTIONS.length - 1) {
      index++;
      renderQuestion();
      scrollToTop();
    }
    return;
  }

  if (reviewCorrectAnswerMode) {
    if (index < QUESTIONS.length - 1) {
      index++;
      renderQuestion();
      scrollToTop();
      return;
    }
    showFinalScore();
    return;
  }

  // In Continue Unanswered mode, the main Next button should still move
  // question-by-question in the current order. Only the Unanswered button
  // jumps to the next unanswered question.
  if (index < QUESTIONS.length - 1) {
    index++;
    renderQuestion();
    scrollToTop();
  } else finishExam();
}

function skipQuestion() {
  if (isStudyMode()) {
    nextQuestion();
    return;
  }

  if (reviewCorrectAnswerMode) {
    nextQuestion();
    return;
  }

  if (continueUnansweredMode) {
    var nextUnanswered = nextUnansweredTargetFrom(index);
    if (nextUnanswered !== -1) {
      index = nextUnanswered;
      renderQuestion();
      scrollToTop();
      return;
    }

    finishExam();
    return;
  }

  nextQuestion();
}
function backQuestion() { if (index > 0) { index--; renderQuestion(); scrollToTop(); } }
function goToQuestion(i) { if (i >= 0 && i < QUESTIONS.length) { if(!reviewCorrectAnswerMode) continueUnansweredMode = false; index = i; renderQuestion(); scrollToTop(); } }
function scrollToTop() { window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' }); }

function getQuestionIdentity(q, fallbackIndex){
  if(q && q._uid) return String(q._uid);
  if(q && typeof q.num !== 'undefined') return String(q.num);
  return String((fallbackIndex || 0) + 1);
}

function getQuestionKeyAt(idx){
  return getQuestionIdentity(QUESTIONS[idx], idx);
}

function visibleFlagCount(){
  var count = 0;
  for(var i = 0; i < QUESTIONS.length; i++){
    var key = getQuestionIdentity(QUESTIONS[i], i);
    if(flagMap[key]) count++;
  }
  return count;
}

function setFlagCountForCurrentPool(){
  var count = 0;

  for(var i = 0; i < QUESTIONS.length; i++){
    var key = getQuestionIdentity(QUESTIONS[i], i);
    if(flagMap[key]) count++;
  }

  var fcEl = byId('flagCount');
  if(fcEl){
    fcEl.textContent = count > 0 ? '⚑ ' + count : '';
    fcEl.style.display = count > 0 ? 'inline-flex' : 'none';
  }
}

function updateStats() {
  if (isStudyMode()) {
    byId('statCorrect').textContent = '--';
    byId('statWrong').textContent = '--';
    byId('statAnswered').textContent = (index + 1) + ' / ' + QUESTIONS.length;

    if(typeof updateTopicUI === 'function') updateTopicUI();
    setFlagCountForCurrentPool();
    return;
  }

  var answered = Object.keys(answeredMap).length;
  var wrong = answered - score;
  byId('statCorrect').textContent = score;
  byId('statWrong').textContent = Math.max(0, wrong);
  byId('statAnswered').textContent = answered + ' / ' + QUESTIONS.length;

  if(typeof updateTopicUI === 'function') updateTopicUI();
  setFlagCountForCurrentPool();
}
function renderJumpButtons() {
  var grid = byId('jumpGrid'); grid.innerHTML = '';
  for (var i = 0; i < QUESTIONS.length; i++) {
    var key = questionKeyAt(i);
    var b = document.createElement('button');
    var cls = 'jump-btn';
    if (i === index) cls += ' active';
    if (answeredMap[key]) cls += resultMap[key] ? ' correct-submitted' : ' wrong-submitted';
    if (flagMap[key]) cls += ' flagged-q';
    b.className = cls;
    b.textContent = i + 1;
    b.setAttribute('data-index', i);
    b.onclick = function(e) {
      e.stopPropagation();

      var targetIndex = parseInt(this.getAttribute('data-index'), 10);
      if(targetIndex === index) return;

      goToQuestion(targetIndex);

      requestAnimationFrame(function(){
        animateSearchJump();
      });
    };
    grid.appendChild(b);
  }
	var fc = Object.keys(flagMap).length;
	var flagEl = byId('flagCount');

	if(fc > 0){
	  flagEl.textContent = '⚑ ' + fc;
	  flagEl.style.display = 'inline-flex';
	}else{
	  flagEl.style.display = 'none';
	}
}
function fisherYates(arr) {
  var a = arr.slice();
  for (var i = a.length - 1; i > 0; i--) { var j = Math.floor(Math.random() * (i + 1)); var t = a[i]; a[i] = a[j]; a[j] = t; }
  return a;
}
function buildShuffledQuestions() {
  var qs = fisherYates(ORIGINAL_QUESTIONS);
  return qs.map(function(q) {
    var orig = ['A','B','C','D']; var shuffled = fisherYates(orig); var newOptions = {}; var optionMap = {};
    shuffled.forEach(function(origLetter, i) { var displayLetter = orig[i]; newOptions[displayLetter] = q.options[origLetter]; optionMap[displayLetter] = origLetter; });
    return Object.assign({}, q, { options: newOptions, _optionMap: optionMap });
  });
}

function getSelectedSectionPool(){
  var full = getFullExamPool().sort(originalQuestionSort);

  if(sectionMode && sectionMode.type === 'range'){
    var startIdx = Math.max(0, Number(sectionMode.start || 1) - 1);
    var endIdx = Math.min(full.length, Number(sectionMode.end || full.length));
    return full.slice(startIdx, endIdx).map(function(q){
      return cloneQuestionOriginal(q);
    });
  }

  return full.map(function(q){
    return cloneQuestionOriginal(q);
  });
}

function getCurrentPoolBaseOrder(){
  var base;

  if(currentQuestionPoolMode === 'flaggedOnly' && flaggedOnlyQuestions && flaggedOnlyQuestions.length){
    base = flaggedOnlyQuestions.slice().sort(originalQuestionSort);
  }else if(currentQuestionPoolMode === 'wrongOnly' && wrongOnlyQuestions && wrongOnlyQuestions.length){
    base = wrongOnlyQuestions.slice().sort(originalQuestionSort);
  }else{
    base = getSelectedSectionPool();
  }

  return base.map(function(q){
    return cloneQuestionOriginal(q);
  });
}

function sectionLabel(start, end){
  if(start === end) return 'Q' + start + ' only';
  return 'Q' + start + ' - Q' + end;
}

function closeSectionModal(){
  var modal = byId('sectionModal');
  if(modal) modal.classList.add('hidden');
  var help = byId('sectionHelpPanel');
  if(help) help.classList.remove('show');
}

function closeSectionShuffleConfirm(){
  var modal = byId('sectionShuffleConfirmModal');
  if(modal) modal.classList.add('hidden');
}

function closeSectionRetakeConfirm(){
  var modal = byId('sectionRetakeConfirmModal');
  if(modal) modal.classList.add('hidden');
}

function confirmExitRetakeAndOpenSection(){
  closeSectionRetakeConfirm();

  currentQuestionPoolMode = 'full';
  wrongOnlyQuestions = null;
  flaggedOnlyQuestions = null;
  flaggedOnlyReturnState = null;

  if(typeof setUiMode === 'function'){
    setUiMode('exam');
  }

  if(fullExamQuestions && fullExamQuestions.length){
    questions = fullExamQuestions.slice();
  }

  renderSectionModal();

  var modal = byId('sectionModal');
  if(modal) modal.classList.remove('hidden');
}

function toggleSectionHelp(){
  var panel = byId('sectionHelpPanel');
  if(panel) panel.classList.toggle('show');
}

function openSectionModal(){
  if(currentQuestionPoolMode === 'wrongOnly'){
    var retakeModal = byId('sectionRetakeConfirmModal');
    if(retakeModal) retakeModal.classList.remove('hidden');
    return;
  }

  if(shuffleMode){
    var warn = byId('sectionShuffleConfirmModal');
    if(warn) warn.classList.remove('hidden');
    return;
  }

  lastSectionListCount = null;
  renderSectionModal();
  var modal = byId('sectionModal');
  if(modal) modal.classList.remove('hidden');
}

function confirmOpenSectionAfterShuffle(){
  closeSectionShuffleConfirm();

  // Section split must start from original order.
  // User can enable shuffle again after choosing the section.
  shuffleMode = false;
  QUESTIONS = restoreQuestionsAndOptions(getCurrentPoolBaseOrder());
  index = 0;

  var btn = byId('shuffleBtn');
  if(btn) btn.classList.remove('on');

  renderQuestion();
  lastSectionListCount = null;
  renderSectionModal();
  var modal = byId('sectionModal');
  if(modal) modal.classList.remove('hidden');
}

function isCurrentSection(start, end){
  if(!sectionMode || sectionMode.type !== 'range') return false;
  return Number(sectionMode.start) === Number(start) && Number(sectionMode.end) === Number(end);
}

function getDefaultSectionSize(total){
  if(sectionMode && sectionMode.type === 'range'){
    var len = Number(sectionMode.end) - Number(sectionMode.start) + 1;
    if(len > 0 && len < total) return len;
  }
  return Math.min(20, total);
}

function compactSectionRange(start, end){
  return start === end ? 'Q' + start : 'Q' + start + '–' + end;
}

function renderSectionButtonsForSize(size, total){
  var html = '';
  var sectionNo = 1;

  for(var start = 1; start <= total; start += size){
    var end = Math.min(start + size - 1, total);
    var active = isCurrentSection(start, end) ? ' active' : '';
    html +=
      '<button class="section-option' + active + '" type="button" onclick="applySectionRange(' + start + ',' + end + ')">' +
        '<span class="section-index">S' + sectionNo + '</span>' +
        '<span class="section-range">' + compactSectionRange(start, end) + '</span>' +
        '<span class="section-option-sub">' + (end - start + 1) + ' Qns</span>' +
      '</button>';
    sectionNo++;
  }

  return html;
}

function renderSectionSizeButton(value, label, activeValue){
  var active = Number(activeValue) === Number(value) ? ' active' : '';
  return '<button class="section-size-btn' + active + '" type="button" onclick="selectSectionSize(' + value + ')">' + label + '</button>';
}

function renderSectionModal(){
  var body = byId('sectionModalBody');
  if(!body) return;

  var total = (QUESTION_BANKS[currentTopic] || []).length;
  var fullActive = (!sectionMode || sectionMode.type === 'full') ? ' active' : '';
  var presets = [10, 20, 40, 60, 80, 100].filter(function(size){ return size < total; });
  var activeSize = Number(sectionPickerSize || getDefaultSectionSize(total));
  if(!activeSize || activeSize < 5 || activeSize > total) activeSize = getDefaultSectionSize(total);
  sectionPickerSize = activeSize;

  var html =
    '<div class="section-picker-sticky">' +

      '<div class="confirm-badge">Section</div>' +

      '<div class="section-title-row">' +
        '<div class="confirm-title">Choose practice section</div>' +
        '<button class="section-help-btn" type="button" onclick="toggleSectionHelp()" aria-label="Section help">?</button>' +
      '</div>' +

      '<div class="section-help-panel" id="sectionHelpPanel">' +
        '<p>Pick the question count first, then choose the section. Shuffle only works inside the selected section.</p>' +
        '<p>Use − / + or quick buttons. Only this breakdown is shown below.</p>' +
      '</div>' +

      '<div class="section-info">Total: ' + total + ' Questions</div>' +

      '<div class="section-grid">' +
        '<button class="section-option' + fullActive + '" type="button" onclick="applyFullSection()">' +
          '<span class="section-index">ALL</span>' +
          '<span class="section-range">Full Exam</span>' +
          '<span class="section-option-sub">' + total + ' Qns</span>' +
        '</button>' +
      '</div>' +

      '<div class="section-group-title">Questions per section</div>' +

      '<div class="section-stepper">' +
        '<button class="section-stepper-btn" type="button" onclick="adjustSectionSize(-5)" aria-label="Decrease questions per section">−</button>' +
        '<div class="section-stepper-value">' + activeSize + '<small>Qns</small></div>' +
        '<button class="section-stepper-btn" type="button" onclick="adjustSectionSize(5)" aria-label="Increase questions per section">+</button>' +
      '</div>' +

      '<div class="section-size-row">';

  presets.forEach(function(size){
    html += renderSectionSizeButton(size, size, activeSize);
  });

  html +=
      '</div>' +
      '<div class="section-group-title">Sections</div>' +
    '</div>' +

    '<div id="sectionList" class="section-grid section-list-grid">' +
      renderSectionButtonsForSize(activeSize, total) +
    '</div>';

  body.innerHTML = html;

  var sectionList = byId('sectionList');
  var sectionCount = Math.ceil(total / activeSize);

  if(sectionList){
    sectionList.classList.remove('section-grow', 'section-shrink');

    if(lastSectionListCount !== null){
      if(sectionCount > lastSectionListCount){
        sectionList.classList.add('section-grow');
      }else if(sectionCount < lastSectionListCount){
        sectionList.classList.add('section-shrink');
      }
    }

    var items = sectionList.querySelectorAll('.section-option');
    items.forEach(function(item, i){
      item.style.animationDelay = Math.min(i * 18, 120) + 'ms';
    });
  }

  lastSectionListCount = sectionCount;
}

function selectSectionSize(size){
  var total = (QUESTION_BANKS[currentTopic] || []).length;
  size = parseInt(size, 10);
  if(!size || size < 1 || size > total) return;
  sectionPickerSize = size;
  renderSectionModal();
}

function adjustSectionSize(delta){
  var total = (QUESTION_BANKS[currentTopic] || []).length;
  var size = parseInt(sectionPickerSize || getDefaultSectionSize(total), 10);
  if(!size) size = Math.min(20, total);

  size += Number(delta || 0);
  size = Math.max(5, Math.min(total, size));

  sectionPickerSize = size;
  renderSectionModal();
}

function applyCustomSectionSize(){
  var input = byId('customSectionSize');
  if(!input) return;

  var total = (QUESTION_BANKS[currentTopic] || []).length;
  var size = parseInt(input.value, 10);

  if(!size || size < 1 || size > total){
    input.value = '';
    input.placeholder = '1 - ' + total;
    return;
  }

  sectionPickerSize = size;
  renderSectionModal();
}

function applyFullSection(){
  sectionMode = { type:'full', start:1, end:null, label:'Full' };
  currentQuestionPoolMode = 'full';
  wrongOnlyQuestions = null;
  flaggedOnlyQuestions = null;
  flaggedOnlyReturnState = null;
  shuffleMode = false;
  closeSectionModal();
  startFreshSessionFromCurrentPool();
}

function applySectionRange(start, end){
  sectionMode = {
    type:'range',
    start:Number(start),
    end:Number(end),
    label:sectionLabel(Number(start), Number(end))
  };
  currentQuestionPoolMode = 'full';
  wrongOnlyQuestions = null;
  flaggedOnlyQuestions = null;
  flaggedOnlyReturnState = null;
  shuffleMode = false;
  closeSectionModal();
  startFreshSessionFromCurrentPool();
}

function refreshAfterReorderKeepProgress(){
  index = 0;

  var result = byId('resultCard');
  if(result){
    result.classList.remove('show');
    result.innerHTML = '';
  }

  byId('questionCard').classList.remove('hidden');
  byId('controlsWrap').classList.remove('hidden');

  renderQuestion();

  if(typeof renderJumpGrid === 'function') renderJumpGrid();
  if(typeof updateStats === 'function') updateStats();

  scrollToTop();
}


function originalQuestionSort(a, b){
  var an = (a && typeof a.num !== 'undefined') ? Number(a.num) : 999999;
  var bn = (b && typeof b.num !== 'undefined') ? Number(b.num) : 999999;
  if(an !== bn) return an - bn;
  return 0;
}

function orderedOptionLetters(options){
  var preferred = ['A','B','C','D','E','F','G','H'];
  var keys = Object.keys(options || {}).map(function(k){ return String(k).toUpperCase(); });
  var out = [];

  preferred.forEach(function(letter){
    if(keys.indexOf(letter) !== -1) out.push(letter);
  });

  keys.forEach(function(letter){
    if(out.indexOf(letter) === -1) out.push(letter);
  });

  return out;
}

function cloneQuestionOriginal(q){
  var tempOptions = {};

  if(q && q._optionMap){
    Object.keys(q.options || {}).forEach(function(displayLetter){
      var originalLetter = q._optionMap[displayLetter] || displayLetter;
      tempOptions[String(originalLetter).toUpperCase()] = q.options[displayLetter];
    });
  }else{
    Object.keys(q.options || {}).forEach(function(letter){
      tempOptions[String(letter).toUpperCase()] = q.options[letter];
    });
  }

  // Rebuild the options object in A/B/C/D order.
  // This fixes the BDCA-style key order after restoring from shuffled options.
  var originalOptions = {};
  orderedOptionLetters(tempOptions).forEach(function(letter){
    originalOptions[letter] = tempOptions[letter];
  });

  var clean = Object.assign({}, q);
  clean.options = originalOptions;
  delete clean._optionMap;

  return clean;
}

function shuffleQuestionOptions(q){
  var clean = cloneQuestionOriginal(q);
  var displayLetters = orderedOptionLetters(clean.options);
  var originalLetters = displayLetters.slice();

  var shuffledOriginalLetters = originalLetters.slice();
  shuffleArray(shuffledOriginalLetters);

  var newOptions = {};
  var optionMap = {};

  for(var i = 0; i < displayLetters.length; i++){
    var displayLetter = displayLetters[i];
    var originalLetter = shuffledOriginalLetters[i];

    newOptions[displayLetter] = clean.options[originalLetter];
    optionMap[displayLetter] = originalLetter;
  }

  var out = Object.assign({}, clean);
  out.options = newOptions;
  out._optionMap = optionMap;

  return out;
}

function restoreQuestionOptions(q){
  return cloneQuestionOriginal(q);
}

function shuffleQuestionsAndOptions(pool){
  var out = pool.slice().map(function(q){
    return shuffleQuestionOptions(q);
  });

  shuffleArray(out);
  return out;
}

function restoreQuestionsAndOptions(pool){
  return pool.slice().map(function(q){
    return restoreQuestionOptions(q);
  });
}

function toggleShuffle(){
  var wasStudy = isStudyMode();
  shuffleMode = !shuffleMode;

  var basePool = getCurrentPoolBaseOrder();

  if(shuffleMode){
    QUESTIONS = shuffleQuestionsAndOptions(basePool);
  }else{
    QUESTIONS = restoreQuestionsAndOptions(basePool);
  }

  var btn = byId('shuffleBtn');
  if(btn){
    if(shuffleMode) btn.classList.add('on');
    else btn.classList.remove('on');
  }

  if(wasStudy){
    selectedMap = {};
    answeredMap = {};
    resultMap = {};
    score = 0;
    if(typeof setUiMode === 'function') setUiMode('study');
  }else if(reviewCorrectAnswerMode){
    if(typeof setUiMode === 'function') setUiMode('summary');
  }else if(currentQuestionPoolMode === 'wrongOnly'){
    if(typeof setUiMode === 'function') setUiMode('retake');
  }else{
    if(typeof setUiMode === 'function') setUiMode('exam');
  }

  index = 0;

  var result = byId('resultCard');
  if(result){
    result.classList.remove('show');
    result.innerHTML = '';
  }

  byId('questionCard').classList.remove('hidden');
  byId('controlsWrap').classList.remove('hidden');

  renderQuestion();

  requestAnimationFrame(function(){
    animateShuffleRefresh();
  });

  if(typeof renderJumpGrid === 'function') renderJumpGrid();
  if(typeof updateStats === 'function') updateStats();
  if(typeof setFlagCountForCurrentPool === 'function') setFlagCountForCurrentPool();

  scrollToTop();
}
function toggleFlag() {
  var key = getQuestionIdentity(QUESTIONS[index], index);

  if (flagMap[key]) delete flagMap[key];
  else flagMap[key] = true;

  if(currentQuestionPoolMode === 'flaggedOnly'){
    refreshFlaggedOnlyAfterFlagChange();
    return;
  }

  renderQuestion();
  if(typeof renderJumpGrid === 'function') renderJumpGrid();
  if(typeof updateStats === 'function') updateStats();
  setFlagCountForCurrentPool();
}
function searchQuestion() {
  var wrap = byId('headerSearchWrap');
  if (wrap && !wrap.classList.contains('open')) {
    toggleSearchPanel();
    return;
  }
  var query = byId('searchInput').value.trim().toLowerCase();
  closeDropdown();
  if (!query) return;

  /*
    Number search should follow the visible Jump table number.
    - When shuffled, Jump buttons show shuffled position numbers (1, 2, 3...)
    - So searching "5" should go to the 5th visible shuffled question, not original Q5
  */
  if (/^\d+$/.test(query)) {
    var n = parseInt(query, 10);
    if (n >= 1 && n <= QUESTIONS.length) {
      goToQuestion(n - 1);
      requestAnimationFrame(function(){
        animateSearchJump();
      });
      hideSearchPanel();
      return;
    }
  }

  var matches = [];
  for (var i = 0; i < QUESTIONS.length; i++) {
    if (JSON.stringify(QUESTIONS[i]).toLowerCase().indexOf(query) !== -1) matches.push(i);
  }
  if (matches.length === 0) {
    byId('answerNote').textContent = 'No match found.';
    return;
  }
  if (matches.length === 1) {
    goToQuestion(matches[0]);
    requestAnimationFrame(function(){
      animateSearchJump();
    });
    hideSearchPanel();
    return;
  }
  showDropdown(matches, query);
}
function showDropdown(matches, query) {
  closeDropdown(); var anchor = byId('dropdownAnchor'); var dd = document.createElement('div'); dd.id = 'searchDropdown';
  var hdr = document.createElement('div'); hdr.style.cssText = 'padding:8px 12px;font-size:11px;color:var(--dim);border-bottom:1px solid var(--b1);'; hdr.textContent = matches.length + ' results for "' + query + '"'; dd.appendChild(hdr);
  matches.forEach(function(i) {
    var q = QUESTIONS[i]; var item = document.createElement('div'); item.className = 'search-result-item'; item.style.cssText = 'padding:10px 12px;border-bottom:1px solid var(--b1);display:flex;gap:10px;cursor:pointer;';
    var num = document.createElement('span'); num.style.cssText = 'font-family:var(--mono);font-size:10px;font-weight:700;color:var(--blue);flex-shrink:0;min-width:24px;'; num.textContent = 'Q' + (i + 1);
    var txt = document.createElement('span'); txt.style.cssText = 'font-size:12px;color:var(--dim);line-height:1.4;overflow:hidden;display:-webkit-box;-webkit-line-clamp:2;-webkit-box-orient:vertical;'; txt.textContent = q.question.replace(/\n/g, ' ');
    item.appendChild(num); item.appendChild(txt); item.onclick = function() {
      goToQuestion(i);
      requestAnimationFrame(function(){
        animateSearchJump();
      });
      closeDropdown();
      hideSearchPanel();
    }; dd.appendChild(item);
  });
  anchor.appendChild(dd);
}
function closeDropdown() { var dd = document.getElementById('searchDropdown'); if (dd) dd.parentNode.removeChild(dd); }
function clearSearch() { byId('searchInput').value = ''; byId('searchInput').focus(); closeDropdown(); }
function toggleSearchPanel() {
  var wrap = byId('headerSearchWrap');
  var btn = byId('searchToggleBtn');
  if (!wrap) return;
  var isOpen = wrap.classList.toggle('open');
  if (btn) btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', isOpen ? 'true' : 'false');
  if (isOpen) {
    setTimeout(function(){ byId('searchInput').focus(); }, 0);
  } else {
    closeDropdown();
  }
}
function hideSearchPanel() {
  var wrap = byId('headerSearchWrap');
  var btn = byId('searchToggleBtn');
  if (wrap) wrap.classList.remove('open');
  if (btn) btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
  closeDropdown();
}
function getJumpPanelHeightBounds() {
  var viewport = window.innerHeight || document.documentElement.clientHeight || 600;
  return {
    min: 16,
    max: Math.max(150, Math.round(viewport * 0.62))
  };
}
function clampJumpPanelBodyHeight(height) {
  var bounds = getJumpPanelHeightBounds();
  var value = Number(height) || bounds.min;
  return Math.min(bounds.max, Math.max(bounds.min, Math.round(value)));
}
function applyJumpPanelBodyHeight(height) {
  var body = byId('jumpPanelBody');
  if (!body) return;
  jumpPanelBodyHeight = clampJumpPanelBodyHeight(height);
  body.style.setProperty('--jump-panel-body-height', jumpPanelBodyHeight + 'px');
}
function resetJumpPanelBodyHeight() {
  var body = byId('jumpPanelBody');
  jumpPanelBodyHeight = null;
  if (body) body.style.removeProperty('--jump-panel-body-height');
}
function getJumpPanelBodyHeight() {
  var body = byId('jumpPanelBody');
  if (!body) return getJumpPanelHeightBounds().min;
  if (jumpPanelBodyHeight !== null) return jumpPanelBodyHeight;

  var rect = body.getBoundingClientRect();
  if (rect.height > 0) return rect.height;

  var viewport = window.innerHeight || document.documentElement.clientHeight || 600;
  return Math.round(viewport * 0.24);
}
function setJumpPanelOpen(open) {
  jumpOpen = !!open;

  var panel = byId('jumpPanel');
  var body = byId('jumpPanelBody');
  var btn = byId('jumpToggle');

  if (panel) {
    panel.classList.toggle('open', jumpOpen);
    if (!jumpOpen) panel.classList.remove('resizing');
  }

  if (body) {
    if (jumpOpen) {
      body.classList.remove('collapsed');
      if (jumpPanelBodyHeight !== null) applyJumpPanelBodyHeight(jumpPanelBodyHeight);
    } else {
      body.classList.add('collapsed');
    }
  }

  if (btn) {
    btn.textContent = jumpOpen ? '\u25b2' : '\u25bc';
    btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', jumpOpen ? 'true' : 'false');
  }
}
function toggleJump() {
  setJumpPanelOpen(!jumpOpen);
}
function updateJumpPanelResize(e) {
  if (jumpResizePointerId !== null && e.pointerId !== jumpResizePointerId) return;
  e.preventDefault();
  var nextHeight = jumpResizeStartHeight + (jumpResizeStartY - e.clientY);
  var bounds = getJumpPanelHeightBounds();

  jumpResizeShouldClose = nextHeight <= bounds.min;
  applyJumpPanelBodyHeight(nextHeight);
}
function endJumpPanelResize(e) {
  if (jumpResizePointerId !== null && e.pointerId !== jumpResizePointerId) return;

  var dragTarget = byId('jumpPanelHeader');
  var panel = byId('jumpPanel');

  if (dragTarget && dragTarget.releasePointerCapture && jumpResizePointerId !== null) {
    try { dragTarget.releasePointerCapture(jumpResizePointerId); } catch (err) {}
  }

  jumpResizePointerId = null;
  if (panel) panel.classList.remove('resizing');

  if (jumpResizeShouldClose) {
    jumpResizeShouldClose = false;
    resetJumpPanelBodyHeight();
    setJumpPanelOpen(false);
  }

  document.removeEventListener('pointermove', updateJumpPanelResize);
  document.removeEventListener('pointerup', endJumpPanelResize);
  document.removeEventListener('pointercancel', endJumpPanelResize);
}
function startJumpPanelResize(e) {
  var body = byId('jumpPanelBody');
  var dragTarget = byId('jumpPanelHeader');
  var panel = byId('jumpPanel');

  if (e.target && e.target.closest && e.target.closest('#jumpToggle')) return;
  if (!jumpOpen || !body || body.classList.contains('collapsed')) return;

  e.preventDefault();
  jumpResizePointerId = e.pointerId;
  jumpResizeStartY = e.clientY;
  jumpResizeStartHeight = getJumpPanelBodyHeight();
  jumpResizeShouldClose = false;

  if (dragTarget && dragTarget.setPointerCapture) dragTarget.setPointerCapture(e.pointerId);
  if (panel) panel.classList.add('resizing');

  document.addEventListener('pointermove', updateJumpPanelResize);
  document.addEventListener('pointerup', endJumpPanelResize);
  document.addEventListener('pointercancel', endJumpPanelResize);
}
function handleJumpPanelResizeKey(e) {
  if (!jumpOpen) return;
  if (e.key !== 'ArrowUp' && e.key !== 'ArrowDown') return;

  e.preventDefault();
  var step = e.shiftKey ? 40 : 16;
  var direction = e.key === 'ArrowUp' ? 1 : -1;
  var nextHeight = getJumpPanelBodyHeight() + (step * direction);

  if (nextHeight <= getJumpPanelHeightBounds().min) {
    resetJumpPanelBodyHeight();
    setJumpPanelOpen(false);
    return;
  }

  applyJumpPanelBodyHeight(nextHeight);
}
function initJumpPanelResize() {
  var header = byId('jumpPanelHeader');
  if (!header || header.getAttribute('data-resize-ready') === '1') return;

  header.setAttribute('data-resize-ready', '1');
  header.addEventListener('pointerdown', startJumpPanelResize);
  header.addEventListener('keydown', handleJumpPanelResizeKey);

  window.addEventListener('resize', function() {
    if (jumpPanelBodyHeight !== null) applyJumpPanelBodyHeight(jumpPanelBodyHeight);
  });
}
function resetState() {
  index = 0;
  score = 0;
  answeredMap = {};
  selectedMap = {};
  resultMap = {};
  continueUnansweredMode = false;
  // flagMap is intentionally kept.
}
function restartQuiz() {
  if(typeof setUiMode === 'function') setUiMode('exam');

  currentQuestionPoolMode = 'full';
  wrongOnlyQuestions = null;
  flaggedOnlyQuestions = null;
  flaggedOnlyReturnState = null;

  var basePool = getCurrentPoolBaseOrder();

  QUESTIONS = shuffleMode
    ? shuffleQuestionsAndOptions(basePool)
    : restoreQuestionsAndOptions(basePool);

  clearAttemptState();

  renderQuestion();
  if(typeof renderJumpGrid === 'function') renderJumpGrid();
  if(typeof updateStats === 'function') updateStats();
  if(typeof setFlagCountForCurrentPool === 'function') setFlagCountForCurrentPool();

  scrollToTop();
}

function findDisplayLetterForOriginal(q, originalLetter) {
  var original = String(originalLetter || '').toLowerCase();
  var keys = Object.keys(q.options || {});

  for (var i = 0; i < keys.length; i++) {
    var display = keys[i];
    var mapped = q._optionMap && q._optionMap[display]
      ? q._optionMap[display]
      : display;

    if (String(mapped).toLowerCase() === original) {
      return display;
    }
  }

  return original.toUpperCase();
}

function answerText(q, letters) {
  if (!letters || letters.length === 0) return 'Not answered';
  return letters.map(function(letter) {
    var display = findDisplayLetterForOriginal(q, letter);
    var text = q.options && q.options[display] ? q.options[display] : '';
    return display.toUpperCase() + '. ' + text;
  }).join(' / ');
}

function summaryStatusClass(key) {
  if (!answeredMap[key]) return 'unanswered';
  return resultMap[key] ? 'correct' : 'wrong';
}

function summaryStatusText(key) {
  if (!answeredMap[key]) return 'Unanswered';
  return resultMap[key] ? 'Correct' : 'Wrong';
}

function buildSummaryOptions(q, key) {
  var selected = selectedMap[key] || [];
  var correct = correctAnswers(q);
  var html = '';

  Object.keys(q.options || {}).forEach(function(displayLetter) {
    var originalLetter = ((q._optionMap && q._optionMap[displayLetter]) ? q._optionMap[displayLetter] : displayLetter).toLowerCase();
    var isCorrect = correct.indexOf(originalLetter) !== -1;
    var isSelected = selected.indexOf(originalLetter) !== -1;

    var cls = 'summary-option';
    if (isCorrect) cls += ' correct-opt';
    else if (isSelected) cls += ' wrong-opt';

    var note = '';
    if (isCorrect && isSelected) note = 'Correct';
    else if (isCorrect) note = 'Answer';
    else if (isSelected) note = 'Your Pick';

    html += '<div class="' + cls + '">' +
      '<span class="summary-letter">' + escHtml(displayLetter.toUpperCase()) + '</span>' +
      '<span>' + formatRichText(q.options[displayLetter]) + '</span>' +
    '</div>';
  });

  return html;
}

function stripRichTags(text){
  return String(text || '')
    .replace(/\[code\]/g, '')
    .replace(/\[\/code\]/g, '')
    .replace(/\[i\]/g, '')
    .replace(/\[\/i\]/g, '')
	.replace(/\[hl\]/g, '')
    .replace(/\[\/hl\]/g, '');
}

function toggleSummaryOptions(btn) {
  var item = btn.closest('.summary-item');
  if (!item) return;

  item.classList.toggle('open');

  var correct = item.querySelector('.summary-correct');
  if (correct) {
    correct.style.display = item.classList.contains('open')
      ? 'none'
      : 'block';
  }

  btn.setAttribute(
    'aria-expanded',
    item.classList.contains('open') ? 'true' : 'false'
  );
}

function questionKeyForSummary(q, idx) {
  if (q && q._uid) return q._uid;
  if (q && typeof q.num !== 'undefined') return String(q.num);
  return String(idx + 1);
}

function buildSummaryOptionsWithSelected(q, key, selectedSourceMap) {
  var selected = (selectedSourceMap && selectedSourceMap[key]) ? selectedSourceMap[key] : [];
  var correct = correctAnswers(q);
  var html = '';

  Object.keys(q.options || {}).forEach(function(displayLetter) {
    var originalLetter = ((q._optionMap && q._optionMap[displayLetter]) ? q._optionMap[displayLetter] : displayLetter).toLowerCase();
    var isCorrect = correct.indexOf(originalLetter) !== -1;
    var isSelected = selected.indexOf(originalLetter) !== -1;

    var cls = 'summary-option';
    if (isCorrect) cls += ' correct-opt';
    else if (isSelected) cls += ' wrong-opt';

    var note = '';
    if (isCorrect && isSelected) note = 'Correct';
    else if (isCorrect) note = 'Answer';
    else if (isSelected) note = 'Your Pick';

    html += '<div class="' + cls + '">' +
      '<span class="summary-letter">' + escHtml(displayLetter.toUpperCase()) + '</span >' +
      '<span class="opt-text-summary">' + formatRichText(q.options[displayLetter]) + '</span>' +
    '</div>';
  });

  return html;
}

function buildSummaryCorrectPreview(q){
  var letters = correctAnswers(q);

  return letters.map(function(letter){
    var displayLetter = findDisplayLetterForOriginal(q, letter);
    var answerText = q.options && q.options[displayLetter]
      ? stripRichTags(q.options[displayLetter])
      : '';

    return '<span class="summary-correct-answer">' +
      escHtml(displayLetter.toUpperCase() + '. ' + answerText) +
    '</span>';
  }).join('');
}

function buildExamSummary(summaryQuestions, summaryAnsweredMap, summaryResultMap, summarySelectedMap) {
  var qList = summaryQuestions || QUESTIONS;
  var aMap = summaryAnsweredMap || answeredMap;
  var rMap = summaryResultMap || resultMap;
  var sMap = summarySelectedMap || selectedMap;

  var html = '<div class="summary-section"><div class="summary-title">Exam Summary</div><div class="summary-list">';
  var itemCount = 0;

  for (var i = 0; i < qList.length; i++) {
    var q = qList[i];
    var key = questionKeyForSummary(q, i);

    var isAnswered = !!aMap[key];
    var isCorrect = !!rMap[key];

    // Summary only shows questions that need review:
    // - wrong answered questions
    // - unanswered questions
    // Correct answered questions are hidden.
	if (isAnswered && isCorrect) {
      continue;
    }
    itemCount++;

    var statusCls = !isAnswered ? 'unanswered' : 'wrong';
    var statusText = !isAnswered ? 'Unanswered' : 'Wrong';
    var correctText = answerText(q, correctAnswers(q));

    html += '<div class="summary-item">' +
      '<button class="summary-head" type="button" onclick="toggleSummaryOptions(this)" aria-expanded="false">' +
        '<span class="summary-main">' +
          '<span class="summary-row">' +
            '<span class="summary-qn">Question ' + (i + 1) + '</span>' +
            '<span class="summary-status ' + statusCls + '">' + escHtml(statusText) + '</span>' +
          '</span>' +
          '<div class="summary-question" style="margin:4px 0 3px;">' + formatSummaryQuestionWithDiagram(q) + '</div>' +
          '<span class="summary-correct" style="margin:13px 0 0px;"><strong>Correct: </strong>' + buildSummaryCorrectPreview(q) + '</span>' +
        '</span>' +
        '<span class="summary-arrow">›</span>' +
      '</button>' +
      '<div class="summary-options">' + buildSummaryOptionsWithSelected(q, key, sMap) + '</div>' +
    '</div>';
  }

  html += '</div></div>';

  if (itemCount === 0) {
    return '<div class="summary-section"><div class="summary-title">Exam Summary</div>' +
      '<div class="summary-item" style="padding:14px 12px;color:var(--green);font-size:13px;">No questions available for this summary.</div></div>';
  }

  return html;
}

function finishExam() {
  var answered = Object.keys(answeredMap).length;
  if (answered < QUESTIONS.length) {
    showFinishConfirm(answered, QUESTIONS.length);
    return;
  }
  continueUnansweredMode = false;
  showFinalScore();
}

function showFinishConfirm(answered, total) {
  var missing = total - answered;
  var msg =
    'You answered ' +
    '<span class="confirm-highlight">' + answered + ' / ' + total + '</span>' +
    ' questions.<br>' +
    '<span class="confirm-warning">' + missing + ' question' + (missing === 1 ? ' is' : 's are') + '</span>' +
    ' still unanswered.<br><br>' +
    'You can continue unanswered questions, or view the exam summary now.';
  byId('finishConfirmText').innerHTML = msg;
  byId('finishConfirmModal').classList.remove('hidden');
}

function closeFinishConfirm() {
  byId('finishConfirmModal').classList.add('hidden');
}

function startContinueUnansweredPractice() {
  closeFinishConfirm();

  var firstMissing = firstUnansweredIndex();
  if (firstMissing === -1) {
    continueUnansweredMode = false;
    showFinalScore();
    return;
  }

  continueUnansweredMode = true;
  index = firstMissing;
  renderQuestion();
  scrollToTop();
}

function showInfoModal(badge, title, html, buttonText){
  var modal = byId('infoModal');
  if(!modal) return;

  var badgeEl = byId('infoModalBadge');
  var titleEl = byId('infoModalTitle');
  var textEl = byId('infoModalText');
  var btnEl = byId('infoModalBtn');

  if(badgeEl) badgeEl.textContent = badge || 'Notice';
  if(titleEl) titleEl.textContent = title || 'Notice';
  if(textEl) textEl.innerHTML = html || '';
  if(btnEl) btnEl.textContent = buttonText || 'OK';

  modal.classList.remove('hidden');
}

function closeInfoModal(){
  var modal = byId('infoModal');
  if(modal) modal.classList.add('hidden');
}

function confirmFinishExam() {
  closeFinishConfirm();
  continueUnansweredMode = false;
  showFinalScore();
}

function returnToReview() {
  var source = lastResultSnapshot || {
    questions: QUESTIONS.slice(),
    answeredMap: Object.assign({}, answeredMap),
    selectedMap: Object.assign({}, selectedMap),
    resultMap: Object.assign({}, resultMap),
    flagMap: Object.assign({}, flagMap),
    score: score,
    poolMode: currentQuestionPoolMode,
    shuffleMode: shuffleMode,
    sectionMode: Object.assign({}, sectionMode)
  };

  reviewCorrectAnswerMode = true;
  continueUnansweredMode = false;

  QUESTIONS = source.questions.slice();
  answeredMap = Object.assign({}, source.answeredMap || {});
  selectedMap = Object.assign({}, source.selectedMap || {});
  resultMap = Object.assign({}, source.resultMap || {});
  flagMap = Object.assign({}, source.flagMap || flagMap || {});
  score = Number(source.score || 0);
  currentQuestionPoolMode = source.poolMode || currentQuestionPoolMode || 'full';
  shuffleMode = !!source.shuffleMode;
  if(source.sectionMode) sectionMode = Object.assign({}, source.sectionMode);

  if(typeof setUiMode === 'function') setUiMode('summary');

  var result = byId('resultCard');
  if (result) {
    result.classList.remove('show');
    result.innerHTML = '';
  }

  byId('questionCard').classList.remove('hidden');
  byId('controlsWrap').classList.remove('hidden');

  var resumeIndex = Number(correctAnswerReviewResumeIndex || 0);
  if(!isFinite(resumeIndex)) resumeIndex = 0;
  index = Math.min(Math.max(0, resumeIndex), Math.max(0, QUESTIONS.length - 1));
  renderQuestion();
  if(typeof renderJumpGrid === 'function') renderJumpGrid();
  if(typeof updateStats === 'function') updateStats();
  if(typeof updateTopicUI === 'function') updateTopicUI();

  scrollToTop();
}


function updateFlaggedOnlyMenuLabel(){
  var btn = byId('moreFlaggedOnlyBtn');
  if(!btn) return;

  var label = btn.querySelector('.menu-label');
  if(!label) return;

  label.textContent = currentQuestionPoolMode === 'flaggedOnly'
    ? 'Show All Questions'
    : 'Show Flagged Only';
}

function getFlaggedQuestionsFromCurrentPool(){
  var list = [];

  for(var i = 0; i < QUESTIONS.length; i++){
    var q = QUESTIONS[i];
    var key = getQuestionIdentity(q, i);
    if(flagMap[key]) list.push(q);
  }

  return list;
}

function startFlaggedOnlyMode(){
  if(currentQuestionPoolMode === 'flaggedOnly'){
    exitFlaggedOnlyMode();
    return;
  }

  var flagged = getFlaggedQuestionsFromCurrentPool();

  if(flagged.length === 0){
    showInfoModal(
      'Flagged',
      'No flagged questions yet',
      'Tap the <span class="confirm-warning">flag icon</span> on any question first, then you can review all flagged questions here.',
      'Got it'
    );
    return;
  }

  flaggedOnlyReturnState = {
    questions: QUESTIONS.slice(),
    index: index,
    poolMode: currentQuestionPoolMode,
    uiMode: currentUiMode,
    wrongOnlyQuestions: wrongOnlyQuestions ? wrongOnlyQuestions.slice() : null,
    sectionMode: sectionMode ? Object.assign({}, sectionMode) : null
  };

  currentQuestionPoolMode = 'flaggedOnly';
  flaggedOnlyQuestions = flagged.slice();
  if(typeof setUiMode === 'function') setUiMode('flagged');

  QUESTIONS = flagged.slice();
  index = 0;

  renderQuestion();
  if(typeof renderJumpGrid === 'function') renderJumpGrid();
  if(typeof updateStats === 'function') updateStats();
  if(typeof updateTopicUI === 'function') updateTopicUI();
  if(typeof setFlagCountForCurrentPool === 'function') setFlagCountForCurrentPool();
  updateFlaggedOnlyMenuLabel();
  scrollToTop();
}

function exitFlaggedOnlyMode(){
  if(!flaggedOnlyReturnState){
    currentQuestionPoolMode = 'full';
    flaggedOnlyQuestions = null;
    flaggedOnlyReturnState = null;
    if(typeof setUiMode === 'function') setUiMode('exam');
    startFreshSessionFromCurrentPool();
    updateFlaggedOnlyMenuLabel();
    return;
  }

  QUESTIONS = flaggedOnlyReturnState.questions.slice();
  index = Math.min(flaggedOnlyReturnState.index || 0, QUESTIONS.length - 1);
  currentQuestionPoolMode = flaggedOnlyReturnState.poolMode || 'full';
  currentUiMode = flaggedOnlyReturnState.uiMode || 'exam';
  wrongOnlyQuestions = flaggedOnlyReturnState.wrongOnlyQuestions ? flaggedOnlyReturnState.wrongOnlyQuestions.slice() : null;
  if(flaggedOnlyReturnState.sectionMode) sectionMode = Object.assign({}, flaggedOnlyReturnState.sectionMode);

  flaggedOnlyQuestions = null;
  flaggedOnlyReturnState = null;

  renderQuestion();
  if(typeof renderJumpGrid === 'function') renderJumpGrid();
  if(typeof updateStats === 'function') updateStats();
  if(typeof updateTopicUI === 'function') updateTopicUI();
  if(typeof setFlagCountForCurrentPool === 'function') setFlagCountForCurrentPool();
  updateFlaggedOnlyMenuLabel();
  scrollToTop();
}

function refreshFlaggedOnlyAfterFlagChange(){
  var source = flaggedOnlyQuestions && flaggedOnlyQuestions.length
    ? flaggedOnlyQuestions.slice()
    : QUESTIONS.slice();

  var currentQuestion = QUESTIONS[index];
  var currentId = currentQuestion ? getQuestionIdentity(currentQuestion, index) : null;

  var refreshed = [];
  for(var i = 0; i < source.length; i++){
    var q = source[i];
    var key = getQuestionIdentity(q, i);
    if(flagMap[key]) refreshed.push(q);
  }

  if(refreshed.length === 0){
    exitFlaggedOnlyMode();
    showInfoModal(
      'Flagged',
      'No flagged questions left',
      'All flags were cleared, so the practice view has returned to <span class="confirm-highlight">all questions</span>.',
      'Continue'
    );
    return;
  }

  flaggedOnlyQuestions = refreshed.slice();
  QUESTIONS = refreshed.slice();

  var nextIndex = 0;
  if(currentId && flagMap[currentId]){
    for(var j = 0; j < QUESTIONS.length; j++){
      if(getQuestionIdentity(QUESTIONS[j], j) === currentId){
        nextIndex = j;
        break;
      }
    }
  }else{
    nextIndex = Math.min(index, QUESTIONS.length - 1);
  }

  index = Math.min(nextIndex, QUESTIONS.length - 1);

  renderQuestion();
  if(typeof renderJumpGrid === 'function') renderJumpGrid();
  if(typeof updateStats === 'function') updateStats();
  if(typeof updateTopicUI === 'function') updateTopicUI();
  if(typeof setFlagCountForCurrentPool === 'function') setFlagCountForCurrentPool();
  updateFlaggedOnlyMenuLabel();
}

var wrongOnlyMode = false;
var wrongOnlySourceQuestions = null;

function getRetakeBuckets(source){
  source = source || lastResultSnapshot || {
    questions: QUESTIONS.slice(),
    answeredMap: Object.assign({}, answeredMap),
    resultMap: Object.assign({}, resultMap)
  };

  var buckets = { wrong: [], unanswered: [], all: [] };

  for (var i = 0; i < source.questions.length; i++) {
    var q = source.questions[i];
    var key = questionKeyForSummary(q, i);
    var isAnswered = !!(source.answeredMap && source.answeredMap[key]);
    var isCorrect = !!(source.resultMap && source.resultMap[key]);

    if (!isAnswered) {
      buckets.unanswered.push(q);
      buckets.all.push(q);
    } else if (!isCorrect) {
      buckets.wrong.push(q);
      buckets.all.push(q);
    }
  }

  return buckets;
}

function getRetakeButtonCounts(source){
  var buckets = getRetakeBuckets(source);
  return {
    wrong: buckets.wrong.length,
    unanswered: buckets.unanswered.length,
    all: buckets.all.length
  };
}

function startRetakePractice(filterMode) {
  var source = lastResultSnapshot || {
    questions: QUESTIONS.slice(),
    answeredMap: Object.assign({}, answeredMap),
    resultMap: Object.assign({}, resultMap)
  };

  var buckets = getRetakeBuckets(source);
  var reviewQuestions = buckets.all;
  var emptyBadge = 'All Correct';
  var emptyTitle = 'No retake needed';
  var emptyMessage = 'Great job — there are no <span class="confirm-warning">wrong or unanswered questions</span> to review.<br><br>You can review the summary or practice the full paper again.';

  if (filterMode === 'wrong') {
    reviewQuestions = buckets.wrong;
    emptyBadge = 'Wrong';
    emptyTitle = 'No wrong questions left';
    emptyMessage = 'There are no <span class="confirm-warning">wrong questions</span> left in this layer.<br><br>You can focus unanswered questions, review the summary, or start the full paper again.';
  } else if (filterMode === 'unanswered') {
    reviewQuestions = buckets.unanswered;
    emptyBadge = 'Unanswered';
    emptyTitle = 'No unanswered questions left';
    emptyMessage = 'There are no <span class="confirm-warning">unanswered questions</span> left in this layer.<br><br>You can focus wrong questions, review the summary, or start the full paper again.';
  }

  if (reviewQuestions.length === 0) {
    if (typeof showInfoModal === 'function') {
      showInfoModal(emptyBadge, emptyTitle, emptyMessage, 'Got it');
    }
    return;
  }

  currentQuestionPoolMode = 'wrongOnly';
  if(typeof setUiMode === 'function') setUiMode('retake');

  // Stored base for Retake mode.
  // Used when user toggles Shuffle OFF, so leftover questions return to JSON original order.
  wrongOnlyQuestions = reviewQuestions
    .map(function(q){ return cloneQuestionOriginal(q); })
    .sort(originalQuestionSort);

  // First Retake screen preserves the result-page order.
  // If the finished paper was shuffled, this keeps that shuffled leftover order.
  QUESTIONS = reviewQuestions.slice();

  selectedMap = {};
  answeredMap = {};
  resultMap = {};
  score = 0;
  index = 0;

  var result = byId('resultCard');
  if(result){
    result.classList.remove('show');
    result.innerHTML = '';
  }

  byId('questionCard').classList.remove('hidden');
  byId('controlsWrap').classList.remove('hidden');

  renderQuestion();
  if(typeof renderJumpGrid === 'function') renderJumpGrid();
  if(typeof updateStats === 'function') updateStats();
  if(typeof updateTopicUI === 'function') updateTopicUI();
  if(typeof setFlagCountForCurrentPool === 'function') setFlagCountForCurrentPool();

  scrollToTop();
}

function startWrongOnlyPractice() {
  startRetakePractice('all');
}

function startRemainingWrongPractice() {
  startRetakePractice('wrong');
}

function startRemainingUnansweredPractice() {
  startRetakePractice('unanswered');
}


function setShuffleButtonState(isOn){
  shuffleMode = !!isOn;

  var shuffleBtn = byId('shuffleBtn');
  if(shuffleBtn){
    if(shuffleMode) shuffleBtn.classList.add('on');
    else shuffleBtn.classList.remove('on');
  }
}

function openRepeatModeModal(){
  var modal = byId('repeatModeModal');
  var badge = byId('repeatModeBadge');
  var title = byId('repeatModeTitle');
  var text = byId('repeatModeText');
  var sameTitle = byId('repeatSameTitle');
  var sameDesc = byId('repeatSameDesc');
  var shuffleTitle = byId('repeatShuffleTitle');
  var shuffleDesc = byId('repeatShuffleDesc');

  if(currentQuestionPoolMode === 'wrongOnly'){
    if(badge) badge.textContent = 'Retake Mode';
    if(title) title.textContent = 'Repeat retake session?';
    if(text) text.textContent = 'Choose whether to keep the current retake order or reshuffle this retake set before restarting.';

    if(sameTitle) sameTitle.textContent = 'Same Retake Order';
    if(sameDesc) sameDesc.textContent = 'Clear answers and restart this retake set using the same order.';

    if(shuffleTitle) shuffleTitle.textContent = 'Shuffle Retake Order';
    if(shuffleDesc) shuffleDesc.textContent = 'Shuffle only this retake question set and restart from Q1.';
  }else{
    if(badge) badge.textContent = 'Practice Again';
    if(title) title.textContent = 'How do you want to repeat?';
    if(text) text.textContent = 'Choose whether to keep the current question order or reshuffle before restarting.';

    if(sameTitle) sameTitle.textContent = 'Same Order';
    if(sameDesc) sameDesc.textContent = 'Clear answers and restart using the current question order.';

    if(shuffleTitle) shuffleTitle.textContent = 'New Shuffle';
    if(shuffleDesc) shuffleDesc.textContent = 'Shuffle this practice set again and restart from Q1.';
  }

  if(modal) modal.classList.remove('hidden');
}

function closeRepeatModeModal(){
  var modal = byId('repeatModeModal');
  if(modal) modal.classList.add('hidden');
}

function openFullPaperModeModal(){
  var modal = byId('fullPaperModeModal');
  if(modal) modal.classList.remove('hidden');
}

function closeFullPaperModeModal(){
  var modal = byId('fullPaperModeModal');
  if(modal) modal.classList.add('hidden');
}

function renderPracticeStartAfterRepeat(){
  var result = byId('resultCard');
  if(result){
    result.classList.remove('show');
    result.innerHTML = '';
  }

  byId('questionCard').classList.remove('hidden');
  byId('controlsWrap').classList.remove('hidden');

  renderQuestion();
  if(typeof renderJumpGrid === 'function') renderJumpGrid();
  if(typeof updateStats === 'function') updateStats();
  if(typeof updateTopicUI === 'function') updateTopicUI();
  if(typeof setFlagCountForCurrentPool === 'function') setFlagCountForCurrentPool();

  scrollToTop();
}

function applyRepeatSourceMode(source){
  currentQuestionPoolMode = source.poolMode || currentQuestionPoolMode || 'full';

  if(currentQuestionPoolMode === 'wrongOnly'){
    if(typeof setUiMode === 'function') setUiMode('retake');
    wrongOnlyQuestions = source.questions
      .map(function(q){ return cloneQuestionOriginal(q); })
      .sort(originalQuestionSort);
  }else{
    if(typeof setUiMode === 'function') setUiMode('exam');
    currentQuestionPoolMode = 'full';
    wrongOnlyQuestions = null;
  }
}

function resetAttemptOnly(){
  reviewCorrectAnswerMode = false;
  continueUnansweredMode = false;
  selectedMap = {};
  answeredMap = {};
  resultMap = {};
  score = 0;
  index = 0;
}

function confirmRepeatSameOrder(){
  closeRepeatModeModal();

  var source = lastResultSnapshot || {
    questions: QUESTIONS.slice(),
    poolMode: currentQuestionPoolMode,
    shuffleMode: shuffleMode
  };

  applyRepeatSourceMode(source);
  setShuffleButtonState(!!source.shuffleMode);

  // Keep the exact displayed question and option order from the completed session.
  QUESTIONS = source.questions.slice();

  resetAttemptOnly();
  renderPracticeStartAfterRepeat();
}

function confirmRepeatNewShuffle(){
  closeRepeatModeModal();

  var source = lastResultSnapshot || {
    questions: QUESTIONS.slice(),
    poolMode: currentQuestionPoolMode
  };

  applyRepeatSourceMode(source);
  setShuffleButtonState(true);

  QUESTIONS = shuffleQuestionsAndOptions(getCurrentPoolBaseOrder());

  resetAttemptOnly();
  renderPracticeStartAfterRepeat();
}

function getPreviousFullPaperSource(){
  var fullLength = getFullExamPool().length;

  if(lastFullPaperSnapshot &&
     lastFullPaperSnapshot.questions &&
     lastFullPaperSnapshot.questions.length === fullLength){
    return lastFullPaperSnapshot;
  }

  return {
    questions: getFullExamPool().sort(originalQuestionSort),
    poolMode: 'full',
    shuffleMode: false,
    sectionMode: { type:'full', start:1, end:null, label:'Full' }
  };
}

function enterFullPaperMode(){
  currentQuestionPoolMode = 'full';
  wrongOnlyQuestions = null;
  flaggedOnlyQuestions = null;
  flaggedOnlyReturnState = null;
  sectionMode = { type:'full', start:1, end:null, label:'Full' };

  if(typeof setUiMode === 'function') setUiMode('exam');
}

function confirmFullPaperPreviousOrder(){
  closeFullPaperModeModal();

  var source = getPreviousFullPaperSource();

  enterFullPaperMode();
  setShuffleButtonState(!!source.shuffleMode);

  // Keep the previous full-paper displayed order when available.
  QUESTIONS = source.questions.slice();

  resetAttemptOnly();
  renderPracticeStartAfterRepeat();
}

function confirmFullPaperNewShuffle(){
  closeFullPaperModeModal();

  enterFullPaperMode();
  setShuffleButtonState(true);

  QUESTIONS = shuffleQuestionsAndOptions(getFullExamPool().sort(originalQuestionSort));

  resetAttemptOnly();
  renderPracticeStartAfterRepeat();
}


function scrollSummaryToTop(){
  var startY = window.scrollY || window.pageYOffset || 0;
  if(startY <= 0) return;

  var duration = 280; // Fast but still visible
  var startTime = null;

  function easeOutCubic(t){
    return 1 - Math.pow(1 - t, 3);
  }

  function animateScroll(timestamp){
    if(!startTime) startTime = timestamp;

    var elapsed = timestamp - startTime;
    var progress = Math.min(elapsed / duration, 1);
    var eased = easeOutCubic(progress);

    window.scrollTo(0, Math.round(startY * (1 - eased)));

    if(progress < 1){
      requestAnimationFrame(animateScroll);
    }
  }

  requestAnimationFrame(animateScroll);
}

function scrollToExamSummary(){
  var summary = document.querySelector('#resultCard .summary-section');
  if(summary){
    summary.scrollIntoView({ behavior:'smooth', block:'start' });
  }else{
    scrollToTop();
  }
}

function updateSummaryTopButton(){
  var btn = byId('summaryTopBtn');
  if(!btn) return;

  var isSummary = currentUiMode === 'summary';
  var shouldShow = isSummary && window.scrollY > 320;

  if(shouldShow) btn.classList.add('show');
  else btn.classList.remove('show');
}

window.addEventListener('scroll', updateSummaryTopButton, { passive:true });

function showFinalScore(options) {
  options = options || {};
  if(!options.preserveCorrectReviewIndex) correctAnswerReviewResumeIndex = 0;

  reviewCorrectAnswerMode = false;
  continueUnansweredMode = false;
  if(typeof setUiMode === 'function') setUiMode('summary');

  var resultQuestions = QUESTIONS.slice();
  var resultAnsweredMap = Object.assign({}, answeredMap);
  var resultSelectedMap = Object.assign({}, selectedMap);
  var resultResultMap = Object.assign({}, resultMap);
  var resultFlagMap = Object.assign({}, flagMap);
  var resultScore = score;

  lastResultSnapshot = {
    questions: resultQuestions,
    answeredMap: resultAnsweredMap,
    selectedMap: resultSelectedMap,
    resultMap: resultResultMap,
    flagMap: resultFlagMap,
    score: resultScore,
    poolMode: currentQuestionPoolMode,
    shuffleMode: shuffleMode,
    sectionMode: Object.assign({}, sectionMode)
  };

  if(currentQuestionPoolMode !== 'wrongOnly'){
    lastFullPaperSnapshot = Object.assign({}, lastResultSnapshot, {
      questions: resultQuestions.slice()
    });
  }

  var answered = Object.keys(resultAnsweredMap).length;
  var wrong = answered - resultScore;
  var unanswered = resultQuestions.length - answered;
