  var pct = Math.round((resultScore / resultQuestions.length) * 100);

  byId('questionCard').classList.add('hidden');
  byId('controlsWrap').classList.add('hidden');

  var result = byId('resultCard');
  result.classList.add('show');

  var flaggedList = Object.keys(resultFlagMap).sort(function(a,b){return Number(a)-Number(b);}).map(function(k){ return 'Q' + k; }).join(', ');

  var summaryHtml = '';
  try {
    summaryHtml = buildExamSummary(resultQuestions, resultAnsweredMap, resultResultMap, resultSelectedMap);
  } catch (err) {
    summaryHtml =
      '<div class="summary-section"><div class="summary-title">Exam Summary</div>' +
      '<div class="summary-item" style="padding:14px 12px;color:var(--red);font-size:13px;">Summary could not be displayed: ' +
      escHtml(err && err.message ? err.message : String(err)) +
      '</div></div>';
  }

  var repeatLabel = (sectionMode && sectionMode.type === 'range') ? '↻ Repeat Section' : '↻ Repeat Full Exam';
  var retakeCounts = getRetakeButtonCounts(lastResultSnapshot);
  var retakeActionsHtml = '';

  if(currentQuestionPoolMode === 'wrongOnly') {
    if(retakeCounts.all > 0) {
      retakeActionsHtml += '<button class="result-action-btn wrong" onclick="startWrongOnlyPractice()">Practice Remaining (' + retakeCounts.all + ')</button>';
      retakeActionsHtml += '<button class="result-action-btn repeat" onclick="openRepeatModeModal()">↻ Repeat This Layer</button>';
      retakeActionsHtml += '<button class="result-action-btn wrong" onclick="openFullPaperModeModal()">📄 Start Full Paper</button>';
    } else {
      retakeActionsHtml += '<button class="result-action-btn wrong" onclick="openFullPaperModeModal()">📄 Start Full Paper</button>';
      retakeActionsHtml += '<button class="result-action-btn repeat" onclick="openRepeatModeModal()">↻ Repeat Retake</button>';
    }
  } else {
    if(retakeCounts.all > 0) {
      retakeActionsHtml += '<button class="result-action-btn wrong" onclick="startWrongOnlyPractice()">Practice Wrong + Unanswered (' + retakeCounts.all + ')</button>';
    }
    retakeActionsHtml += '<button class="result-action-btn repeat" onclick="openRepeatModeModal()">↻ Practice Again</button>';
  }

  result.innerHTML =
    '<div class="result-badge">FINAL RESULT</div>' +
    '<div class="result-score">' + pct + '<span class="result-denom">%</span></div>' +
    '<div class="result-raw">Correct: ' + resultScore + ' / ' + resultQuestions.length + '</div>' +
    '<div class="result-verdict ' + (pct >= 50 ? 'verdict-pass' : 'verdict-fail') + '">' + (pct >= 50 ? 'PASS' : 'REVIEW') + '</div>' +
    '<div class="result-stats">' +
      '<div class="rs"><div class="rs-v" style="color:var(--green)">' + resultScore + '</div><div class="rs-l">Correct</div></div>' +
      '<div class="rs"><div class="rs-v" style="color:var(--red)">' + Math.max(0, wrong) + '</div><div class="rs-l">Wrong</div></div>' +
      '<div class="rs"><div class="rs-v" style="color:var(--amber)">' + unanswered + '</div><div class="rs-l">Unanswered</div></div>' +
    '</div>' +
    (flaggedList ? '<div style="color:var(--amber);font-size:12px;margin-bottom:14px;">⚑ Flagged: ' + escHtml(flaggedList) + '</div>' : '') +
    '<div class="result-actions">' +
      '<button class="result-action-btn review" onclick="returnToReview()">View Correct Answers</button>' +
      retakeActionsHtml +
    '</div>' +
    summaryHtml +
	  '<button class="summary-top-btn" id="summaryTopBtn" type="button" onclick="scrollSummaryToTop()" aria-label="Back to top">' +
		'<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" aria-hidden="true">' +
		  '<polygon points="16,14 6,24 7.4,25.4 16,16.8 24.6,25.4 26,24"/>' +
		  '<rect x="4" y="8" width="24" height="2"/>' +
		'</svg>' +
	  '</button>';

  updateSummaryTopButton();
  scrollToTop();
  setTimeout(updateSummaryTopButton, 60);
}
function backToSummaryFromReview(){
  correctAnswerReviewResumeIndex = Math.max(0, Number(index || 0));
  reviewCorrectAnswerMode = false;
  continueUnansweredMode = false;
  showFinalScore({ preserveCorrectReviewIndex:true });
}

byId('submitBtn').onclick = function() {
  if (isStudyMode()) {
    if (index < QUESTIONS.length - 1) {
      animateQuestionChange('next', nextQuestion);
    } else {
      openStudyExitConfirm();
    }
    return;
  }

  if (reviewCorrectAnswerMode) {
    backToSummaryFromReview();
    return;
  }

  if (answeredMap[currentKey()]) {
    if (index === QUESTIONS.length - 1) {
      finishExam();
    } else {
      animateQuestionChange('next', nextQuestion);
    }
  } else {
    submitAnswer();
  }
};
byId('searchInput').addEventListener('keydown', function(e) { if (e.key === 'Enter') searchQuestion(); });
document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
  var dd = document.getElementById('searchDropdown');
  var wrap = byId('headerSearchWrap');
  var toggle = byId('searchToggleBtn');
  var insideSearch = wrap && wrap.contains(e.target);
  var onToggle = toggle && toggle.contains(e.target);
  if (dd && !dd.contains(e.target) && !insideSearch && !onToggle) closeDropdown();
  if (wrap && wrap.classList.contains('open') && !insideSearch && !onToggle && !byId('searchInput').value.trim()) hideSearchPanel();
});
updateTopicUI();
if(typeof updateFlaggedOnlyMenuLabel === 'function') updateFlaggedOnlyMenuLabel();
if (!document.body.classList.contains('home-mode')) renderQuestion();

(function setupMoreMenu(){
  var moreBtn = document.getElementById('moreBtn');
  var moreMenu = document.getElementById('moreMenu');
  var restartBtn = document.getElementById('moreRestartBtn');
  var clearFlagsBtn = document.getElementById('moreClearFlagsBtn');
  var flaggedOnlyBtn = document.getElementById('moreFlaggedOnlyBtn');
  var studyToggleBtn = document.getElementById('moreStudyToggleBtn');
  var toggleJumpBtn = document.getElementById('moreToggleJumpBtn');

  if(moreBtn && moreMenu){
    moreBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e){
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
      updateStudyToggleMenuItem();
      moreMenu.classList.toggle('hidden');
    });

    moreMenu.addEventListener('click', function(e){
      e.stopPropagation();
    });

    document.addEventListener('click', function(){
      moreMenu.classList.add('hidden');
    });
  }

  if(restartBtn){
    restartBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e){
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();

      if(typeof openResetProgressConfirm === 'function'){
        openResetProgressConfirm();
      }
    });
  }

  if(studyToggleBtn){
    studyToggleBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e){
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
      toggleStudyModeFromMore();
    });
  }

  if(flaggedOnlyBtn){
    flaggedOnlyBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e){
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();

      if(moreMenu) moreMenu.classList.add('hidden');

      if(typeof startFlaggedOnlyMode === 'function'){
        startFlaggedOnlyMode();
      }
    });
  }

  if(clearFlagsBtn){
    clearFlagsBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e){
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();

      flagMap = {};

      if(moreMenu) moreMenu.classList.add('hidden');

      if(currentQuestionPoolMode === 'flaggedOnly' && typeof exitFlaggedOnlyMode === 'function'){
        exitFlaggedOnlyMode();
        return;
      }

      if(typeof renderJumpGrid === 'function'){
        renderJumpGrid();
      }
      if(typeof renderQuestion === 'function'){
        renderQuestion();
      }
      if(typeof updateStats === 'function'){
        updateStats();
      }
    });
  }

  if(toggleJumpBtn){
    toggleJumpBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e){
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();

      if(moreMenu) moreMenu.classList.add('hidden');

      if(typeof toggleJump === 'function'){
        toggleJump();
      }
    });
  }
})();

function openResetProgressConfirm(){
  var modal = byId('restartConfirmModal');
  if(modal) modal.classList.remove('hidden');

  var menu = byId('moreMenu');
  if(menu) menu.classList.add('hidden');
}

function closeResetProgressConfirm(){
  var modal = byId('restartConfirmModal');
  if(modal) modal.classList.add('hidden');
}

function resetCurrentAttemptKeepOrder(){
  var wasStudy = isStudyMode();

  // Reset Progress must leave answer-review / continue-unanswered modes.
  // It clears answer progress only; flags and the current question order are kept.
  reviewCorrectAnswerMode = false;
  continueUnansweredMode = false;
  lastResultSnapshot = null;

  // Reset Progress mode normalization:
  // Retake stays RETAKE; summary/review returns to normal exam view.
  if(wasStudy){
    if(typeof setUiMode === 'function') setUiMode('study');
  }else if(currentQuestionPoolMode === 'wrongOnly'){
    if(typeof setUiMode === 'function') setUiMode('retake');
  }else{
    if(typeof setUiMode === 'function') setUiMode('exam');
  }

  // Reset Progress clears only answer progress.
  // Flags are kept because they act like bookmarks.
  selectedMap = {};
  answeredMap = {};
  resultMap = {};
  score = 0;
  index = 0;

  var result = byId('resultCard');
  if(result){
    result.classList.remove('show');
    result.innerHTML = '';
  }

  var qCard = byId('questionCard');
  var controls = byId('controlsWrap');
  if(qCard) qCard.classList.remove('hidden');
  if(controls) controls.classList.remove('hidden');

  renderQuestion();

  if(typeof renderJumpGrid === 'function') renderJumpGrid();
  if(typeof updateStats === 'function') updateStats();

  scrollToTop();
}

function confirmResetProgress(){
  closeResetProgressConfirm();
  resetCurrentAttemptKeepOrder();
}

function shuffleArray(arr){
  for(var i = arr.length - 1; i > 0; i--){
    var j = Math.floor(Math.random() * (i + 1));
    var tmp = arr[i];
    arr[i] = arr[j];
    arr[j] = tmp;
  }
  return arr;
}

function clearAttemptState(){
  reviewCorrectAnswerMode = false;
  continueUnansweredMode = false;

  selectedMap = {};
  answeredMap = {};
  resultMap = {};
  score = 0;
  index = 0;

  // Do not clear flagMap here.
  // Flags are bookmarks and should persist until user manually clicks Clear All Flags.

  var result = byId('resultCard');
  if(result){
    result.classList.remove('show');
    result.innerHTML = '';
  }

  byId('questionCard').classList.remove('hidden');
  byId('controlsWrap').classList.remove('hidden');
}

function getFullExamPool(){
  if(typeof QUESTION_BANKS !== 'undefined' && typeof currentTopic !== 'undefined'){
    return (QUESTION_BANKS[currentTopic] || []).slice().map(function(q){
      return cloneQuestionOriginal(q);
    });
  }

  return QUESTIONS.slice().map(function(q){
    return cloneQuestionOriginal(q);
  }).sort(originalQuestionSort);
}

function rebuildCurrentPoolForShuffle(){
  var basePool = getCurrentPoolBaseOrder();

  QUESTIONS = shuffleMode
    ? shuffleQuestionsAndOptions(basePool)
    : restoreQuestionsAndOptions(basePool);
}

function startFreshSessionFromCurrentPool(){
  var wasStudy = isStudyMode();
  rebuildCurrentPoolForShuffle();
  clearAttemptState();
  if(wasStudy && typeof setUiMode === 'function') setUiMode('study');
  renderQuestion();

  if(typeof renderJumpGrid === 'function') renderJumpGrid();
  if(typeof updateStats === 'function') updateStats();

  scrollToTop();
}

/* mode-badge-init */
if(typeof updateTopicUI === 'function') updateTopicUI();

function formatRichText(text){
  return escHtml(text)
    .replace(/\[i\]/g, '<em>')
    .replace(/\[\/i\]/g, '</em>')
    .replace(/\[code\]/g, '<code>')
    .replace(/\[\/code\]/g, '</code>')
    .replace(/\[hl\]/g, '<span class="hl">')
    .replace(/\[\/hl\]/g, '</span>');
}

function formatQuestionText(text){
  return formatRichText(text);
}

function diagramHtml(q, cls){
  if(!q || !q.diagram) return '';
  var src = String(q.diagram || '');
  if(!/^data:image\//.test(src)) return '';
  return '<div class="' + (cls || 'question-diagram') + '">' +
    '<img src="' + escHtml(src) + '" alt="Question exhibit">' +
    '</div>';
}

function formatTextWithDiagram(q, formatter, cls){
  var text = String((q && q.question) || '');
  var diagram = diagramHtml(q, cls);
  if(!diagram) return formatter(text);
  var match = text.match(/Refer to the exhibit[\\.:]?/i);
  if(!match) return formatter(text) + diagram;
  var splitAt = match.index + match[0].length;
  var before = text.slice(0, splitAt);
  var after = text.slice(splitAt).replace(/^\\s+/, '');
  return formatter(before) + diagram + (after ? formatter(after) : '');
}

function formatQuestionWithDiagram(q){
  return formatTextWithDiagram(q, formatQuestionText, 'question-diagram');
}

function formatSummaryQuestionWithDiagram(q){
  return formatTextWithDiagram(q, formatRichText, 'summary-diagram');
}

</script>

<script>
/* Prevent iOS Safari fast double-tap zoom on repeated taps */
let lastTouchEnd = 0;

document.addEventListener('touchend', function(event){
  const now = Date.now();

  if(now - lastTouchEnd <= 300){
    event.preventDefault();
  }

  lastTouchEnd = now;
}, { passive:false });
</script>
